```mermaid
flowchart TD
    Start[Helm Template Evaluation] --> Cond{admissionWebhooks.create AND<br/>autoGenerateCert.enabled AND<br/>NOT certManager.enabled}
    Cond -->|false| End[Skip Resource Creation]
    Cond -->|true| GenCA[Generate CA Certificate]
    GenCA --> GenCert[Generate Signed Certificate]
    GenCert --> CreateSecret[Create TLS Secret]
    CreateSecret --> CreateMutating[Create MutatingWebhookConfiguration]
    CreateMutating --> CreateValidating[Create ValidatingWebhookConfiguration]
    CreateValidating --> End
```

## Diagram 2

```mermaid
graph TB
    Secret[TLS Secret<br/>kubernetes.io/tls]
    MWC[MutatingWebhookConfiguration]
    VWC[ValidatingWebhookConfiguration]
    WS[Webhook Service]
    
    Secret -->|provides caBundle & TLS| MWC
    Secret -->|provides caBundle & TLS| VWC
    
    MWC --> MW1[minstrumentation.kb.io<br/>Instrumentation Mutator]
    MWC --> MW2[mamazoncloudwatchagent.kb.io<br/>Agent Mutator]
    MWC --> MW3[mpod.kb.io<br/>Pod Mutator]
    MWC --> MW4[mnamespace.kb.io<br/>Namespace Mutator]
    MWC --> MW5[mworkload.kb.io<br/>Workload Mutator]
    
    VWC --> VW1[vinstrumentationcreateupdate.kb.io<br/>Instrumentation Validator CREATE/UPDATE]
    VWC --> VW2[vinstrumentationdelete.kb.io<br/>Instrumentation Validator DELETE]
    VWC --> VW3[vamazoncloudwatchagentcreateupdate.kb.io<br/>Agent Validator CREATE/UPDATE]
    VWC --> VW4[vamazoncloudwatchagentdelete.kb.io<br/>Agent Validator DELETE]
    
    MW1 -.->|calls| WS
    MW2 -.->|calls| WS
    MW3 -.->|calls| WS
    MW4 -.->|calls| WS
    MW5 -.->|calls| WS
    VW1 -.->|calls| WS
    VW2 -.->|calls| WS
    VW3 -.->|calls| WS
    VW4 -.->|calls| WS
```

## Diagram 3

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant K8S as Kubernetes API Server
    participant MWH as Mutating Webhook
    participant VWH as Validating Webhook
    participant WS as Webhook Service
    participant Res as Resource

    K8S->>MWH: Intercept CREATE/UPDATE Request
    MWH->>WS: Forward AdmissionReview
    WS->>WS: Apply Mutations
    WS-->>MWH: Return Patched Resource
    MWH-->>K8S: Continue with Mutations
    K8S->>VWH: Validate Mutated Resource
    VWH->>WS: Forward AdmissionReview
    WS->>WS: Validate Resource
    WS-->>VWH: Return Validation Result
    VWH-->>K8S: Admit or Reject
    K8S->>Res: Create/Update Resource
```

```mermaid
        +caBundle string
    }
    class ServiceReference {
        +name string
        +namespace string
        +path string
    }
    class Secret {
        +type kubernetes.io/tls
        +tls.crt string
        +tls.key string
    }
    
    MutatingWebhookConfiguration "1" --> "*" Webhook
    ValidatingWebhookConfiguration "1" --> "*" Webhook
    Webhook "1" --> "1" ClientConfig
    ClientConfig "1" --> "1" ServiceReference
    Secret ..> ClientConfig : provides caBundle
```
